## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the canonical form of population dynamics ODEs. The relationship captures how birth, death, competition, and environmental factors determine population change.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth with constant per-capita rate)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth with logarithmic density dependence)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant removal rate)
- Beverton-Holt continuous form: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with hyperbolic saturation)
- Time-varying exponential: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (growth rate changing exponentially with time)
- Logistic with time-dependent capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (seasonally or temporally varying carrying capacity)
- Richards growth model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * P) (reduced growth at low density without extinction threshold)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (growth rate as power of population size)
- Von Bertalanffy type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Oscillatory forcing: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic growth with periodic environmental forcing)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear dependence on P (dP_dt ŌłØ P) ŌåÆ exponential/Malthusian regime indicating no density dependence
- Quadratic polynomial in P (terms P and P┬▓) ŌåÆ logistic-type density-dependent regulation with carrying capacity
- Cubic polynomial in P (terms P, P┬▓, P┬│) ŌåÆ Allee effect with both lower critical threshold and upper carrying capacity
- Logarithmic coupling log(P) multiplied by P ŌåÆ Gompertz-type growth with asymmetric approach to carrying capacity
- Ratio P/(1+cP) structure ŌåÆ contest competition where resources are divided among individuals
- Additive constant term independent of P ŌåÆ external immigration/harvesting independent of population size
- Product of P with trigonometric function of t ŌåÆ seasonal or periodic environmental forcing on reproduction
- Fractional power P**c with 0<c<1 ŌåÆ surface-area-to-volume scaling in organism growth models
- Multiple factors (P-c1)(P-c2) ŌåÆ multiple equilibria corresponding to distinct ecological stable states
- Exponential decay in time multiplied by growth term ŌåÆ transient environmental change or resource depletion
